\subsection*{Game 3: TeX Chess Engine vs Stockfish (1-0)}
\noindent 1.~Nc3 d5 2.~e3 a6 3.~Bd3 e5 4.~Nf3 e4 5.~Bxe4 dxe4 6.~Ng1 Bf5 7.~g4 Be6 8.~Kf1 Nd7 9.~d3 h5 10.~gxh5 exd3 11.~Qxd3 Qh4 12.~Qe4 Qxe4 13.~Nxe4 f5 14.~Nd2 Ngf6 15.~Ne2 Rd8 16.~Nf4 Nc5 17.~b4 Rxd2 18.~Bxd2 Bc4+ 19.~Kg1 Nce4 20.~Ng6 Rxh5 21.~h4 Bd6 22.~Be1 Kf7 23.~f3 Ng5 24.~hxg5 Be2 25.~gxf6 Rxh1+ 26.~Kxh1 Kxg6 27.~fxg7 Bxf3+ 28.~Kg1 Kf7 29.~Bc3 Bg3 30.~b5 f4 31.~bxa6 fxe3 32.~a7 Bh1 33.~a8=Q Bg2 34.~g8=Q+ Ke7 35.~Qad8\# 1-0
